name:j‚Äço‚Äçe‚Äço‚Äçe‚Äçc‚Äçy
info:Superior Double room
info:Stayed in October 2023
info:Other
info:2 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted October 5, 2023
msg:I went back to my hometown during the National Day holiday and visited Hefei. There was no room in Binhu Fumao, so I decided to come to voco (because it was a bit remote).
Transportation: voco is close to Yungu Park on Metro Line 5, 1 km away. It is relatively close to Binhu Yintai and Yuefang. It costs more than 20 yuan to take a Didi taxi to Mixc. It is not very convenient, but I still enjoy the feeling of walking at night. Feel the slow life in Hefei.
Environment: InterContinental is not bad, and it focuses on intelligence. There is a brother to greet you at the door, and the hotel lobby is not inferior to ordinary hotels. Check-in/elevator are all face-scanning. The room is equipped with **all Genie. The sound insulation effect is also very good. The toiletries elemis smell very comfortable. The shower room also uses a push-type switch. The thoughtful thing is the atomized glass, which can adjust the privacy freely. The drinks are free to drink, and there is also tea. The gym and laundry room are together, and you can also enter by face-scanning. Small but exquisite.
Breakfast: There are not many varieties, but they are all quite fresh. The aunties below are all very good. I feel quite relaxed working here (unlike some other hotels)
Overall: Voco in Hefei is very cost-effective and is a good entry-level five-star hotel. I will definitely stay here again.
